-- The <description> section contains the text that will appear in the Set Probe... window.
-- It gives you a chance to describe how the probe works, what the parameters are, and how to
-- how to set it up. 

<description>

\gb\SENSAPHONE-MIB Viewer\p\

This is a probe that will view the entire SENSAPHONE-MIB. The Status Window shows all the scalar values available from the MIB, and also has links to display the tables that are supported.

You must import the following MIBs before importing the probe file.

   RFC1155-SMI
   RFC1213-MIB
   RFC-1212
   RFC-1215
   SENSAPHONE-MIB

</description>
